4. Pham toi trong truong hop co kha nang thuc te dan den hau qua dac biet nghiem trong neu khong duoc ngan chan kip thoi, thi bi phat tien tu ba trieu dong den ba muoi trieu dong, cai tao khong giam giu den mot nam hoac phat tu tu ba thang den hai nam.
Dieu 210. Toi dua vao su dung cac phuong tien giao thong duong sat khong bao dam an toan
1. Nguoi nao chiu trach nhiem truc tiep ve viec dieu dong hoac ve tinh trang ky thuat cua phuong tien giao thong duong sat ma cho phep dua vao su dung phuong tien giao thong duong sat ro rang khong bao dam an toan gay thiet hai cho tinh mang hoac gay thiet hai nghiem trong cho suc khoe, tai san cua nguoi khac hoac da bi xu ly ky luat ve hanh vi nay ma con vi pham, thi bi phat tien tu muoi trieu dong den nam muoi trieu dong, cai tao khong giam giu den ba nam hoac phat tu tu mot nam den nam nam.
2. Pham toi gay hau qua rat nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu ba nam den muoi nam.
3. Pham toi gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu bay nam den muoi lam nam.
4. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi cam dam nhiem chuc vu, cam hanh nghe hoac lam cong viec nhat dinh tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 211. Toi dieu dong hoac giao cho nguoi khong du dieu kien dieu khien cac phuong tien giao thong duong sat 
1. Nguoi nao dieu dong hoac giao cho nguoi khong co giay phep hoac bang lai hoac khong du cac dieu kien khac theo quy dinh cua phap luat chi huy, dieu khien phuong tien giao thong duong sat gay thiet hai cho tinh mang hoac gay thiet hai nghiem trong cho suc khoe, tai san cua nguoi khac hoac da bi xu ly ky luat ve hanh vi nay ma con vi pham, thi bi phat tien tu muoi trieu dong den nam muoi trieu dong, cai tao khong giam giu den ba nam hoac phat tu tu mot nam den nam nam.
2. Pham toi gay hau qua rat nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu ba nam den muoi nam.
3. Pham toi gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu bay nam den muoi lam nam.
4. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi cam dam nhiem chuc vu, cam hanh nghe hoac lam cong viec nhat dinh tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 212. Toi vi pham quy dinh ve dieu khien phuong tien giao thong duong thuy 
1. Nguoi nao dieu khien phuong tien giao thong duong thuy ma vi pham quy dinh ve an toan giao thong duong thuy gay thiet hai cho tinh mang hoac gay thiet hai nghiem trong cho suc khoe, tai san cua nguoi khac, thi bi phat tien tu muoi trieu dong den nam muoi trieu dong, cai tao khong giam giu den ba nam hoac phat tu tu mot nam den nam nam.
2. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu ba nam den muoi nam:
a) Khong co giay phep, bang hoac chung chi chuyen mon tuong uung voi nhiem vu duoc giao;
b) Trong tinh trang dung ruou, bia qua nong do quy dinh hoac say do dung cac chat kich thich manh khac;
c) Gay tai nan roi bo chay de tron tranh trach nhiem hoac co y khong cuu giup nguoi bi nan;
d) Khong chap hanh hieu lenh cua nguoi chi huy hoac nguoi co tham quyen dieu khien, giu gin trat tu, an toan giao thong duong thuy;
d) Gay hau qua rat nghiem trong.
3. Pham toi gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu bay nam den muoi lam nam.
4. Pham toi trong truong hop co kha nang thuc te dan den hau qua dac biet nghiem trong, neu khong duoc ngan chan kip thoi, thi bi phat tien tu nam trieu dong den ba muoi trieu dong, cai tao khong giam giu den hai nam hoac phat tu tu sau thang den ba nam.
5. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi cam dam nhiem chuc vu, cam hanh nghe hoac lam cong viec nhat dinh tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 213. Toi can tro giao thong duong thuy 
1. Nguoi nao co mot trong cac hanh vi sau day can tro giao thong duong thuy gay thiet hai cho tinh mang hoac gay thiet hai nghiem trong cho suc khoe, tai san cua nguoi khac, thi bi phat tien tu muoi trieu dong den nam muoi trieu dong, cai tao khong giam giu den ba nam hoac phat tu tu mot nam den nam nam:
a) Khoan, dao trai phep lam hu hai ket cau cua cac cong trinh giao thong duong thuy;
b) Tao ra chuong ngai vat gay can tro giao thong duong thuy ma khong dat va duy tri bao hieu;
c) Di chuyen lam giam hieu luc, tac dung cua bao hieu;
d) Thao do bao hieu hoac pha hoai cong trinh giao thong duong thuy;
d) Lan chiem luong hoac hanh lang bao ve luong giao thong duong thuy;
e ) Hanh vi khac can tro giao thong duong thuy.
2. Pham toi gay hau qua rat nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu ba nam den muoi nam.
3. Pham toi gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu bay nam den muoi lam nam.
4. Pham toi trong truong hop co kha nang thuc te dan den hau qua dac biet nghiem trong neu khong duoc ngan chan kip thoi, thi bi phat tien tu nam trieu dong den ba muoi trieu dong, cai tao khong giam giu den mot nam hoac phat tu tu ba thang den hai nam.
Dieu 214. Toi dua vao su dung cac phuong tien giao thong duong thuy khong bao dam an toan
1. Nguoi nao chiu trach nhiem truc tiep ve viec dieu dong hoac ve tinh trang ky thuat cua phuong tien giao thong duong thuy ma cho phep dua vao su dung phuong tien giao thong duong thuy ro rang khong bao dam an toan gay thiet hai cho tinh mang hoac gay thiet hai nghiem trong cho suc khoe, tai san cua nguoi khac hoac da bi xu ly ky luat, xu phat hanh chinh ve hanh vi nay hoac da bi ket an ve toi nay, chua duoc xoa an tich ma con vi pham, thi bi phat tien tu muoi trieu dong den nam muoi trieu dong, cai tao khong giam giu den ba nam hoac phat tu tu mot nam den nam nam.
2. Pham toi gay hau qua rat nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu ba nam den muoi nam.
3. Pham toi gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu bay nam den muoi lam nam.
4. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi cam dam nhiem chuc vu, cam hanh nghe hoac lam cong viec nhat dinh tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 215. Toi dieu dong hoac giao cho nguoi khong du dieu kien dieu khien cac phuong tien giao thong duong thuy 
1. Nguoi nao dieu dong hoac giao cho nguoi khong co giay phep hoac bang lai hoac khong du cac dieu kien khac theo quy dinh cua phap luat dieu khien phuong tien giao thong duong thuy gay thiet hai cho tinh mang hoac gay thiet hai nghiem trong cho suc khoe, tai san cua nguoi khac hoac da bi xu ly ky luat, xu phat hanh chinh ve hanh vi nay hoac da bi ket an ve toi nay, chua duoc xoa an tich ma con vi pham, thi bi phat tien tu muoi trieu dong den nam muoi trieu dong, cai tao khong giam giu den ba nam hoac phat tu tu mot nam den nam nam.
2. Pham toi gay hau qua rat nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu ba nam den muoi nam.
3. Pham toi gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu bay nam den muoi lam nam.
4. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi cam dam nhiem chuc vu, cam hanh nghe hoac lam cong viec nhat dinh tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 216. Toi vi pham quy dinh dieu khien tau bay  
1. Nguoi nao chi huy, dieu khien tau bay ma vi pham cac quy dinh ve an toan giao thong duong khong, co kha nang thuc te dan den hau qua dac biet nghiem trong neu khong duoc ngan chan kip thoi, thi bi phat tien tu nam trieu dong den nam muoi trieu dong, cai tao khong giam giu den ba nam hoac phat tu tu mot nam den nam nam.
2. Pham toi gay thiet hai cho tinh mang hoac gay thiet hai nghiem trong cho suc khoe, tai san cua nguoi khac, thi bi phat tu tu ba nam den muoi nam.
3. Pham toi gay hau qua rat nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu bay nam den muoi lam nam.
4. Pham toi gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu muoi hai nam den hai muoi nam.
5. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi cam dam nhiem chuc vu, cam hanh nghe hoac lam cong viec nhat dinh tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 217. Toi can tro giao thong duong khong 
1. Nguoi nao co mot trong cac hanh vi sau day can tro giao thong duong khong gay thiet hai cho tinh mang hoac gay thiet hai nghiem trong cho suc khoe, tai san cua nguoi khac hoac da bi xu ly ky luat, xu phat hanh chinh ve hanh vi nay hoac da bi ket an ve toi nay, chua duoc xoa an tich ma con vi pham, thi bi phat tien tu muoi trieu dong den nam muoi trieu dong, cai tao khong giam giu den ba nam hoac phat tu tu mot nam den nam nam:
a) Dat cac chuong ngai vat can tro giao thong duong khong;
b) Di chuyen trai phep, lam sai lech, che khuat, hoac pha huy cac bien hieu, tin hieu an toan giao thong duong khong;
c) Su dung sai hoac lam nhieu cac tan so thong tin lien lac;
d) Cung cap thong tin sai lac gay nguy hiem cho chuyen bay;
d) Lam hu hong trang thiet bi cua san bay hoac trang thiet bi phu tro khac;
e ) Hanh vi khac can tro giao thong duong khong.
2. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu ba nam den muoi nam:
a) La nguoi co trach nhiem truc tiep bao dam an toan giao thong duong khong hoac truc tiep quan ly cac thiet bi an toan giao thong duong khong;
b) Gay hau qua rat nghiem trong.
3. Pham toi gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu bay nam den muoi lam nam.
4. Pham toi co kha nang thuc te dan den hau qua dac biet nghiem trong, neu khong duoc ngan chan kip thoi, thi bi phat tien tu nam trieu den hai muoi trieu dong, cai tao khong giam giu den ba nam hoac phat tu tu sau thang den ba nam.
5. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi cam dam nhiem chuc vu, cam hanh nghe hoac lam cong viec nhat dinh tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 218. Toi dua vao su dung phuong tien giao thong duong khong khong bao dam an toan
1. Nguoi nao co trach nhiem truc tiep ve viec dieu dong hoac ve tinh trang ky thuat cua cac phuong tien giao thong duong khong ma cho dua vao su dung cac phuong tien ro rang khong bao dam an toan ky thuat, thi bi phat tu tu mot nam den nam nam.
2. Pham toi gay thiet hai cho tinh mang hoac thiet hai nghiem trong cho suc khoe, tai san cua nguoi khac, thi bi phat tu tu ba nam den muoi nam.
3. Pham toi gay hau qua rat nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu tam nam den muoi lam nam.
4. Pham toi gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu muoi hai nam den hai muoi nam.
5. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi cam dam nhiem chuc vu, cam hanh nghe hoac lam cong viec nhat dinh tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 219. Toi dieu dong hoac giao cho nguoi khong du dieu kien dieu khien cac phuong tien giao thong duong khong
1. Nguoi nao dieu dong hoac giao cho nguoi khong co bang lai hoac khong du cac dieu kien khac theo quy dinh cua phap luat dieu khien phuong tien giao thong duong khong, thi bi phat tu tu mot nam den nam nam.
2. Pham toi gay thiet hai cho tinh mang hoac gay thiet hai nghiem trong cho suc khoe, tai san cua nguoi khac, thi bi phat tu tu ba nam den muoi nam.
3. Pham toi gay hau qua rat nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu tam nam den muoi lam nam.
4. Pham toi gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu muoi hai nam den hai muoi nam.
5. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi cam dam nhiem chuc vu, cam hanh nghe hoac lam cong viec nhat dinh tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 220. Toi vi pham quy dinh ve duy tu, sua chua, quan ly cac cong trinh giao thong 
1. Nguoi nao co trach nhiem trong viec duy tu, sua chua, quan ly cac cong trinh giao thong duong bo, duong sat, duong thuy, duong khong ma vi pham cac quy dinh ve duy tu, sua chua, quan ly cac cong trinh do gay thiet hai cho tinh mang hoac gay thiet hai nghiem trong cho suc khoe, tai san cua nguoi khac, thi bi phat tien tu nam trieu dong den mot tram trieu dong, cai tao khong giam giu den ba nam hoac phat tu tu sau thang den ba nam.
2. Pham toi gay hau qua rat nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu hai nam den bay nam.
3. Pham toi gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu nam nam den muoi lam nam.
4. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi phat tien tu nam trieu dong den nam muoi trieu dong, cam dam nhiem chuc vu, cam hanh nghe hoac lam cong viec nhat dinh tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 221. Toi chiem doat tau bay, tau thuy 
1. Nguoi nao dung vu luc, de doa dung vu luc hoac dung cac thu doan khac nham chiem doat tau bay hoac tau thuy, thi bi phat tu tu bay nam den muoi lam nam.
2. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu muoi hai nam den hai muoi nam:
a) Co to chuc;
b) Su dung vu khi hoac phuong tien nguy hiem;
c) Gay thuong tich hoac gay ton hai cho suc khoe cua nguoi khac;
d) Tai pham nguy hiem.
3. Pham toi lam chet nguoi hoac gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong khac, thi bi phat tu hai muoi nam, tu chung than hoac tu hinh.
4. Nguoi pham toi con bi phat quan che hoac cam cu tru tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 222. Toi dieu khien tau bay vi pham cac quy dinh ve hang khong cua nuoc Cong hoa xa hoi chu nghia Viet Nam  
1. Nguoi nao dieu khien tau bay vao hoac ra khoi Viet Nam ma vi pham cac quy dinh ve hang khong cua nuoc Cong hoa xa hoi chu nghia Viet Nam neu khong thuoc truong hop quy dinh tai Dieu 80 va Dieu 81 cua Bo luat nay, thi bi phat tien tu mot tram trieu dong den ba tram trieu dong hoac phat tu tu sau thang den ba nam.
2. Pham toi gay hau qua nghiem trong thi bi phat tien tu ba tram trieu dong den nam tram trieu dong hoac phat tu tu hai nam den bay nam.
3. Pham toi gay hau qua rat nghiem trong hoac dac biet nghiem trong, thi bi phat tien tu nam tram trieu dong den mot ty dong hoac bi phat tu tu nam nam den muoi nam.
4. Phuong tien bay co the bi tich thu.
Dieu 223. Toi dieu khien phuong tien hang hai vi pham cac quy dinh ve hang hai cua nuoc Cong hoa xa hoi chu nghia Viet Nam 
1. Nguoi nao dieu khien tau thuy hay phuong tien hang hai khac vao hoac ra khoi Viet Nam hoac di qua lanh hai Viet Nam ma vi pham cac quy dinh ve hang hai cua nuoc Cong hoa xa hoi chu nghia Viet Nam, neu khong thuoc truong hop quy dinh tai Dieu 80 va Dieu 81 cua Bo luat nay, thi bi phat tien tu nam muoi trieu dong den hai tram trieu dong hoac phat tu tu ba thang den hai nam.
2. Pham toi gay hau qua nghiem trong thi bi phat tien tu hai tram trieu dong den nam tram trieu dong hoac phat tu tu mot nam den ba nam.
3. Pham toi gay hau qua rat nghiem trong hoac dac biet nghiem trong, thi bi phat tien tu nam tram trieu dong den tam tram trieu dong hoac phat tu tu ba nam den bay nam.
4. Phuong tien hang hai co the bi tich thu.
Dieu 224. Toi tao ra va lan truyen, phat tan cac chuong trinh vi - rut tin hoc 
1. Nguoi nao tao ra va co y lan truyen, phat tan cac chuong trinh vi-rut qua mang may tinh hoac bang cac phuong thuc khac gay roi loan hoat dong, phong toa hoac lam bien dang, lam huy hoai cac du lieu cua may tinh hoac da bi xu ly ky luat, xu phat hanh chinh ve hanh vi nay ma con vi pham, thi bi phat tien tu nam trieu dong den mot tram trieu dong hoac phat tu tu sau thang den ba nam.
2. Pham toi gay hau qua rat nghiem trong hoac dac biet nghiem trong, thi bi phat tu tu hai nam den bay nam.
3. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi phat tien tu nam trieu dong den nam muoi trieu dong, cam dam nhiem chuc vu, cam hanh nghe hoac lam cong viec nhat dinh tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 225. Toi vi pham cac quy dinh ve van hanh, khai thac va su dung mang may tinh dien tu
1. Nguoi nao duoc su dung mang may tinh ma vi pham cac quy dinh ve van hanh, khai thac va su dung mang may tinh gay roi loan hoat dong, phong toa hoac lam bien dang, lam huy hoai cac du lieu cua may tinh hoac da bi xu ly ky luat, xu phat hanh chinh ve hanh vi nay ma con vi pham, thi bi phat tien tu nam trieu dong den mot tram trieu dong, cai tao khong giam giu den ba nam hoac phat tu tu mot nam den ba nam.
2. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu hai nam den nam nam:
a) Co to chuc;
b) Gay hau qua rat nghiem trong hoac dac biet nghiem trong.
3. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi phat tien tu nam trieu dong den nam muoi trieu dong, cam dam nhiem chuc vu, cam hanh nghe hoac lam cong viec nhat dinh tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 226. Toi su dung trai phep thong tin tren mang va trong may tinh 
1. Nguoi nao su dung trai phep thong tin tren mang va trong may tinh, cung nhu dua vao mang may tinh nhung thong tin trai voi quy dinh cua phap luat gay hau qua nghiem trong, da bi xu ly ky luat, xu phat hanh chinh ma con vi pham, thi bi phat tien tu nam trieu dong den nam muoi trieu dong, cai tao khong giam giu den ba nam hoac bi phat tu tu sau thang den ba nam.
2. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu hai nam den nam nam:
a) Co to chuc;
b) Gay hau qua rat nghiem trong hoac dac biet nghiem trong.
3. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi phat tien tu ba trieu dong den ba muoi trieu dong, cam dam nhiem chuc vu, cam hanh nghe hoac lam cong viec nhat dinh tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 227. Toi vi pham quy dinh ve an toan lao dong, ve sinh lao dong, ve an toan o  nhung noi dong nguoi  
1. Nguoi nao vi pham quy dinh ve an toan lao dong, ve sinh lao dong, ve an toan o  nhung noi dong nguoi gay thiet hai cho tinh mang hoac gay thiet hai nghiem trong cho suc khoe, tai san cua nguoi khac, thi bi phat cai tao khong giam giu den ba nam hoac phat tu tu sau thang den nam nam.
2. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu ba nam den muoi nam:
a) La nguoi co trach nhiem ve an toan lao dong, ve sinh lao dong, ve an toan o  nhung noi dong nguoi;
b) Gay hau qua rat nghiem trong.
3. Pham toi gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu bay nam den muoi hai nam.
4. Pham toi trong truong hop co kha nang thuc te dan den hau qua dac biet nghiem trong neu khong duoc ngan chan kip thoi, thi bi phat cai tao khong giam giu den ba nam hoac phat tu tu sau thang den ba nam.
5. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi phat tien tu nam trieu den nam muoi trieu dong, cam dam nhiem chuc vu, cam hanh nghe hoac lam cong viec nhat dinh tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 228. Toi vi pham quy dinh ve su dung lao dong tre em 
1. Nguoi nao su dung tre e m lam nhung cong viec nang nhoc, nguy hiem hoac tiep xuc voi cac chat doc hai theo danh muc ma Nha nuoc quy dinh gay hau qua nghiem trong, hoac da bi xu phat hanh chinh ve hanh vi nay ma con vi pham, thi bi phat tien tu nam trieu dong den nam muoi trieu dong, cai tao khong giam giu den hai nam hoac phat tu tu ba thang den hai nam.
2. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu hai nam den bay nam:
a) Pham toi nhieu lan;
b) Doi voi nhieu tre e m;
c) Gay hau qua rat nghiem trong hoac dac biet nghiem trong.
3. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi phat tien tu hai trieu dong den hai muoi trieu dong.
Dieu 229. Toi vi pham quy dinh ve xay dung gay hau qua nghiem trong 
1. Nguoi nao vi pham quy dinh ve xay dung trong cac linh vuc khao sat, thiet ke, thi cong, su dung nguyen lieu, vat lieu, may moc, nghiem thu cong trinh hay cac linh vuc khac neu khong thuoc truong hop quy dinh tai Dieu 220 cua Bo luat nay gay thiet hai cho tinh mang hoac gay thiet hai nghiem trong cho suc khoe, tai san cua nguoi khac, thi bi phat tien tu muoi trieu dong den mot tram trieu dong, cai tao khong giam giu den ba nam hoac phat tu tu sau thang den nam nam.
2. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu ba nam den muoi nam:
a) La nguoi co chuc vu, quyen han;
b) Gay hau qua rat nghiem trong.
3. Pham toi gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu tam nam den hai muoi nam.
4. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi phat tien tu nam trieu dong den nam muoi trieu dong, cam dam nhiem chuc vu, cam hanh nghe hoac lam cong viec nhat dinh tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 230. Toi che tao, tang tru, van chuyen, su dung, mua ban trai phep hoac chiem doat vu khi quan dung, phuong tien ky thuat quan su 
1. Nguoi nao che tao, tang tru, van chuyen, su dung, mua ban trai phep hoac chiem doat vu khi quan dung, phuong tien ky thuat quan su, thi bi phat tu tu mot nam den bay nam.
2. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu nam nam den muoi hai nam:
a) Co to chuc;
b) Vat pham phap co so luong lon;
c) Van chuyen, mua ban qua bien gioi;
d) Gay hau qua nghiem trong;
d) Tai pham nguy hiem.
3. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu muoi nam den muoi lam nam:
a) Vat pham phap co so luong rat lon;
b) Gay hau qua rat nghiem trong.
4. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu muoi lam nam den hai muoi nam hoac tu chung than:
a) Vat pham phap co so luong dac biet lon;
b) Gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong.
5. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi phat tien tu nam trieu dong den nam muoi trieu dong, phat quan che hoac cam cu tru tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 231. Toi pha huy cong trinh, phuong tien quan trong ve an ninh quoc gia 
1. Nguoi nao pha huy cong trinh hoac phuong tien giao thong van tai, thong tin - lien lac, cong trinh dien, dan chat dot, cong trinh thuy loi hoac cong trinh quan trong khac ve an ninh, quoc phong, kinh te, khoa hoc - ky thuat, van hoa va xa hoi, neu khong thuoc truong hop quy dinh tai Dieu 85 cua Bo luat nay, thi bi phat tu tu ba nam den muoi hai nam.
2. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu muoi nam den hai muoi nam, tu chung than hoac tu hinh:
a) Co to chuc;
b) Gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong;
c) Tai pham nguy hiem.
3. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi phat quan che   tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 232. Toi che tao, tang tru, van chuyen, su dung, mua ban trai phep hoac chiem doat vat lieu no   
1. Nguoi nao che tao, tang tru, van chuyen, su dung, mua ban trai phep hoac chiem doat vat lieu no, thi bi phat tu tu mot nam den nam nam.
2. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu ba nam den muoi nam:
a) Co to chuc;
b) Vat pham phap co so luong lon;
c) Van chuyen, mua ban qua bien gioi;
d) Gay hau qua nghiem trong;
d) Tai pham nguy hiem.
3. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu bay nam den muoi lam nam:
a) Vat pham phap co so luong rat lon;
b) Gay hau qua rat nghiem trong.
4. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu muoi lam nam den hai muoi nam hoac tu chung than:
a) Vat pham phap co so luong dac biet lon;
b) Gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong.
5. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi phat tien tu nam trieu dong den nam muoi trieu dong, phat quan che hoac cam cu tru tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 233. Toi che tao, tang tru, van chuyen, su dung, mua ban trai phep hoac chiem doat vu khi tho so hoac cong cu ho tro 
1. Nguoi nao che tao, tang tru, van chuyen, su dung, mua ban trai phep hoac chiem doat vu khi tho so hoac cong cu ho tro, da bi xu phat hanh chinh ve hanh vi nay hoac da bi ket an ve toi nay, chua duoc xoa an tich ma con vi pham, thi bi phat tu tu ba thang den hai nam.
2. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu mot nam den nam nam:
a) Co to chuc;
b) Vat pham phap co so luong lon;
c) Van chuyen, mua ban qua bien gioi;
d) Gay hau qua nghiem trong;
d) Tai pham nguy hiem.
3. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi phat tien tu nam trieu dong den nam muoi trieu dong, phat quan che hoac cam cu tru tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 234. Toi vi pham quy dinh ve quan ly vu khi, vat lieu no, cong cu ho tro 
1. Nguoi nao vi pham quy dinh ve quan ly viec san xuat, sua chua, trang bi, su dung, bao quan, luu giu, van chuyen, mua ban vu khi, vat lieu no, cong cu ho tro gay thiet hai cho tinh mang hoac gay thiet hai nghiem trong cho suc khoe, tai san cua nguoi khac, thi bi phat tu tu mot nam den nam nam.
2. Pham toi gay hau qua rat nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu ba nam den muoi nam.
3. Pham toi gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu muoi nam den muoi lam nam.
4. Pham toi trong truong hop co kha nang thuc te dan den hau qua dac biet nghiem trong neu khong duoc ngan chan kip thoi, thi bi phat cai tao khong giam giu den ba nam hoac phat tu tu sau thang den ba nam.
5. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi cam dam nhiem chuc vu, cam hanh nghe hoac lam cong viec nhat dinh tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 235. Toi thieu trach nhiem trong viec giu vu khi, vat lieu no, cong cu ho tro gay hau qua nghiem trong 
1. Nguoi nao duoc giao vu khi, vat lieu no, cong cu ho tro ma thieu trach nhiem de nguoi khac su dung vu khi, vat lieu no, cong cu ho tro gay thiet hai cho tinh mang hoac gay thiet hai nghiem trong cho suc khoe, tai san cua nguoi khac, thi bi phat cai tao khong giam giu den ba nam hoac phat tu tu sau thang den nam nam.
2. Pham toi gay hau qua rat nghiem trong hoac dac biet nghiem trong, thi bi phat tu tu ba nam den muoi nam.
3. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi cam dam nhiem chuc vu, cam hanh nghe hoac lam cong viec nhat dinh tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 236. Toi san xuat, tang tru, van chuyen, su dung, mua ban trai phep hoac chiem doat chat phong xa 
1. Nguoi nao san xuat, tang tru, van chuyen, su dung, mua ban trai phep hoac chiem doat chat phong xa, thi bi phat tu tu hai nam den bay nam.
2. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu nam nam den muoi hai nam:
a) Co to chuc;
b) Vat pham phap co so luong lon;
c) Van chuyen, mua ban qua bien gioi;
d) Gay hau qua nghiem trong;
d) Tai pham nguy hiem.
3. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu muoi nam den muoi lam nam:
a) Vat pham phap co so luong rat lon;
b) Gay hau qua rat nghiem trong.
4. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu muoi lam nam den hai muoi nam hoac tu chung than:
a) Vat pham phap co so luong dac biet lon;
b) Gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong.
5. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi phat tien tu nam trieu dong den nam muoi trieu dong, phat quan che hoac cam cu tru tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 237. Toi vi pham quy dinh ve quan ly chat phong xa 
1. Nguoi nao vi pham quy dinh ve quan ly viec san xuat, trang bi, su dung, bao quan, luu giu, van chuyen, mua ban chat phong xa, co kha nang thuc te dan den hau qua nghiem trong neu khong duoc ngan chan kip thoi, thi bi phat cai tao khong giam giu den ba nam hoac phat tu tu sau thang den ba nam.
2. Pham toi trong truong hop gay thiet hai cho tinh mang, suc khoe cua nguoi khac, thi bi phat tu tu ba nam den muoi nam.
3. Pham toi gay hau qua rat nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu bay nam den muoi lam nam.
4. Pham toi gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong thi bi phat tu tu muoi lam nam den hai muoi nam.
5. Nguoi pham toi con co the bi cam dam nhiem chuc vu, cam hanh nghe hoac lam cong viec nhat dinh tu mot nam den nam nam.
Dieu 238. Toi san xuat, tang tru, van chuyen, su dung hoac mua ban trai phep chat chay, chat doc 
1. Nguoi nao san xuat, tang tru, van chuyen, su dung, mua ban trai phep chat chay, chat doc, thi bi phat tu tu mot nam den nam nam.
2. Pham toi thuoc mot trong cac truong hop sau day, thi bi phat tu tu ba nam den muoi nam:
a) Co to chuc;
b) Vat pham phap co so luong lon;
c) Van chuyen, mua ban qua bien gioi;
d) Gay hau qua nghiem trong;
d) Tai pham nguy hiem.

a) Vat pham phap co so luong rat lon;
b) Gay hau qua rat nghiem trong.

a) Vat pham phap co so luong dac biet lon;
b) Gay hau qua dac biet nghiem trong.
